Thu Feb  4 10:47:16 2016:   select stop-freeze_time/24-current_timestamp,
         case
           when (current_timestamp-"START")*24<duration then (current_timestamp-"START")*24
           when (current_timestamp-"START")*24>=duration then duration
         end
  from Contests
  where cont_id=110

Thu Feb  4 10:47:16 2016: Tmp_stand called: cont_id=110, isteam=0, isvirt=0, user=0, type=1, master=0
Thu Feb  4 10:47:16 2016:   select Status.id_publ, Cont_prob.pr_num, Status.id_rsl,
        (cast(Status.dt_tm as date)-cast(Contests."START" as date))*24*60+
        (cast(Status.dt_tm as time)-cast(Contests."START" as time))/60 penalty
  from
    (
      (status join cont_status on status.id_stat=cont_status.id_stat and cont_status.cont_id=110)
    join
      cont_prob
    on
      cont_prob.prob_id=status.id_prb and cont_status.cont_id=cont_prob.cont_id
    )
  join
    contests
  on
    contests.cont_id=cont_status.cont_id
  where Status.id_rsl<100 and
        Status.dt_tm-Contests."START">0 and
        Contests.stop-Contests.freeze_time/24-Status.dt_tm>0

  order by Status.id_publ,
           Cont_prob.pr_num,
           Status.dt_tm

Sat Feb  6 19:12:41 2016:   select stop-freeze_time/24-current_timestamp,
         case
           when (current_timestamp-"START")*24<duration then (current_timestamp-"START")*24
           when (current_timestamp-"START")*24>=duration then duration
         end
  from Contests
  where cont_id=110

Sat Feb  6 19:12:41 2016: Tmp_stand called: cont_id=110, isteam=0, isvirt=0, user=0, type=1, master=0
Sat Feb  6 19:12:41 2016:   select Status.id_publ, Cont_prob.pr_num, Status.id_rsl,
        (cast(Status.dt_tm as date)-cast(Contests."START" as date))*24*60+
        (cast(Status.dt_tm as time)-cast(Contests."START" as time))/60 penalty
  from
    (
      (status join cont_status on status.id_stat=cont_status.id_stat and cont_status.cont_id=110)
    join
      cont_prob
    on
      cont_prob.prob_id=status.id_prb and cont_status.cont_id=cont_prob.cont_id
    )
  join
    contests
  on
    contests.cont_id=cont_status.cont_id
  where Status.id_rsl<100 and
        Status.dt_tm-Contests."START">0 and
        Contests.stop-Contests.freeze_time/24-Status.dt_tm>0

  order by Status.id_publ,
           Cont_prob.pr_num,
           Status.dt_tm

Mon Feb  8 06:48:30 2016:   select R.reg_time+C.duration/24-current_timestamp,
         case
           when (current_timestamp-R.reg_time)*24<duration then (current_timestamp-R.reg_time)*24
           when (current_timestamp-R.reg_time)*24>=duration then duration
         end
  from Contests C JOIN Regauth R on C.cont_id=R.cont_id
  where C.cont_id=117 and
        R.user_id=0

Mon Feb  8 06:48:30 2016: Tmp_stand called: cont_id=117, isteam=0, isvirt=1, user=0, type=1, master=0
Mon Feb  8 06:48:30 2016:   select Status.id_publ, Cont_prob.pr_num, Status.id_rsl,
        (cast(Status.dt_tm as date)-cast(Regauth.reg_time as date))*24*60+
        (cast(Status.dt_tm as time)-cast(Regauth.reg_time as time))/60 penalty
  from
    (
      (
        (status join cont_status on status.id_stat=cont_status.id_stat and cont_status.cont_id=117)
      join
        cont_prob
      on
        cont_prob.prob_id=status.id_prb and cont_status.cont_id=cont_prob.cont_id
      )
    join
      contests
    on
      contests.cont_id=cont_status.cont_id
    )
  join
    regauth
  on
    regauth.user_id=status.id_publ and regauth.cont_id=117
  where Status.id_rsl<100 and
        Status.dt_tm-Regauth.reg_time>=0 and
        Status.dt_tm-Regauth.reg_time<(Contests.duration-Contests.freeze_time)/24
                and
        Status.dt_tm-Regauth.reg_time<=
           (
             select current_timestamp-reg_time
             from Regauth
             where cont_id=117 and user_id=0
           )

  order by Status.id_publ,
           Cont_prob.pr_num,
           Status.dt_tm

  from
    (
      (

      join
        cont_prob
      on
        cont_prob.prob_id=status.id_prb and cont_status.cont_id=cont_prob.cont_id
      )
    join
      contests
    on
      contests.cont_id=cont_status.cont_id
    )

    regauth
  on
    regauth.user_id=status.id_publ and regauth.cont_id=116

             from Regauth
             where cont_id=116 and user_id=0
           )

           Cont_prob.pr_num,
           Status.dt_tm

Thu Feb 11 09:38:18 2016:   select Status.id_publ, Cont_prob.pr_num, Status.id_rsl,
        (cast(Status.dt_tm as date)-cast(Contests."START" as date))*24*60+

  from
    (
      (status join cont_status on status.id_stat=cont_status.id_stat and cont_status.cont_id=108)
    join
      cont_prob
    on
      cont_prob.prob_id=status.id_prb and cont_status.cont_id=cont_prob.cont_id
    )

    contests
  on
    contests.cont_id=cont_status.cont_id
  where Status.id_rsl<100 and
        Status.dt_tm-Contests."START">0 and
        Contests.stop-Contests.freeze_time/24-Status.dt_tm>0

  order by Status.id_publ,
           Cont_prob.pr_num,
           Status.dt_tm

Mon Feb 15 10:35:42 2016: Tmp_stand called: cont_id=108, isteam=0, isvirt=0, user=0, type=1, master=0
Mon Feb 15 10:35:42 2016:   select Status.id_publ, Cont_prob.pr_num, Status.id_rsl,
        (cast(Status.dt_tm as date)-cast(Contests."START" as date))*24*60+
        (cast(Status.dt_tm as time)-cast(Contests."START" as time))/60 penalty
  from
    (
      (status join cont_status on status.id_stat=cont_status.id_stat and cont_status.cont_id=108)
    join
      cont_prob
    on
      cont_prob.prob_id=status.id_prb and cont_status.cont_id=cont_prob.cont_id
    )
  join
    contests
  on
    contests.cont_id=cont_status.cont_id
  where Status.id_rsl<100 and
        Status.dt_tm-Contests."START">0 and
        Contests.stop-Contests.freeze_time/24-Status.dt_tm>0

  order by Status.id_publ,
           Cont_prob.pr_num,

Thu Feb 18 16:48:07 2016: Tmp_stand called: cont_id=117, isteam=0, isvirt=1, user=0, type=1, master=0
Thu Feb 18 16:48:07 2016:   select Status.id_publ, Cont_prob.pr_num, Status.id_rsl,
        (cast(Status.dt_tm as date)-cast(Regauth.reg_time as date))*24*60+
        (cast(Status.dt_tm as time)-cast(Regauth.reg_time as time))/60 penalty
  from
    (
      (
        (status join cont_status on status.id_stat=cont_status.id_stat and cont_status.cont_id=117)
      join
        cont_prob
      on
        cont_prob.prob_id=status.id_prb and cont_status.cont_id=cont_prob.cont_id
      )
    join
      contests
    on
      contests.cont_id=cont_status.cont_id
    )
  join
    regauth
  on
    regauth.user_id=status.id_publ and regauth.cont_id=117
  where Status.id_rsl<100 and
        Status.dt_tm-Regauth.reg_time>=0 and
        Status.dt_tm-Regauth.reg_time<(Contests.duration-Contests.freeze_time)/24
                and
        Status.dt_tm-Regauth.reg_time<=
           (
             select current_timestamp-reg_time
             from Regauth
             where cont_id=117 and user_id=0
           )

  order by Status.id_publ,
           Cont_prob.pr_num,
           Status.dt_tm

Sun Feb 21 12:19:01 2016: Tmp_stand called: cont_id=108, isteam=0, isvirt=0, user=0, type=1, master=0
Sun Feb 21 12:19:01 2016:   select Status.id_publ, Cont_prob.pr_num, Status.id_rsl,
        (cast(Status.dt_tm as date)-cast(Contests."START" as date))*24*60+
        (cast(Status.dt_tm as time)-cast(Contests."START" as time))/60 penalty
  from
    (
      (status join cont_status on status.id_stat=cont_status.id_stat and cont_status.cont_id=108)
    join
      cont_prob
    on
      cont_prob.prob_id=status.id_prb and cont_status.cont_id=cont_prob.cont_id
    )
  join
    contests
  on
    contests.cont_id=cont_status.cont_id
  where Status.id_rsl<100 and
        Status.dt_tm-Contests."START">0 and
        Contests.stop-Contests.freeze_time/24-Status.dt_tm>0

  order by Status.id_publ,
           Cont_prob.pr_num,
           Status.dt_tm

Mon Feb 22 02:24:12 2016: Tmp_stand called: cont_id=117, isteam=0, isvirt=1, user=0, type=1, master=0
Mon Feb 22 02:24:12 2016:   select Status.id_publ, Cont_prob.pr_num, Status.id_rsl,
        (cast(Status.dt_tm as date)-cast(Regauth.reg_time as date))*24*60+
        (cast(Status.dt_tm as time)-cast(Regauth.reg_time as time))/60 penalty
  from
    (
      (
        (status join cont_status on status.id_stat=cont_status.id_stat and cont_status.cont_id=117)
      join
        cont_prob
      on
        cont_prob.prob_id=status.id_prb and cont_status.cont_id=cont_prob.cont_id
      )
    join
      contests
    on
      contests.cont_id=cont_status.cont_id
    )
  join
    regauth
  on
    regauth.user_id=status.id_publ and regauth.cont_id=117
  where Status.id_rsl<100 and
        Status.dt_tm-Regauth.reg_time>=0 and
        Status.dt_tm-Regauth.reg_time<(Contests.duration-Contests.freeze_time)/24
                and
        Status.dt_tm-Regauth.reg_time<=
           (
             select current_timestamp-reg_time
             from Regauth
             where cont_id=117 and user_id=0
           )

  order by Status.id_publ,
           Cont_prob.pr_num,
           Status.dt_tm

Tue Feb 23 12:44:09 2016: Tmp_stand called: cont_id=117, isteam=0, isvirt=1, user=0, type=1, master=0
Tue Feb 23 12:44:09 2016:   select Status.id_publ, Cont_prob.pr_num, Status.id_rsl,
        (cast(Status.dt_tm as date)-cast(Regauth.reg_time as date))*24*60+
        (cast(Status.dt_tm as time)-cast(Regauth.reg_time as time))/60 penalty
  from
    (
      (
        (status join cont_status on status.id_stat=cont_status.id_stat and cont_status.cont_id=117)
      join
        cont_prob
      on
        cont_prob.prob_id=status.id_prb and cont_status.cont_id=cont_prob.cont_id
      )
    join
      contests
    on
      contests.cont_id=cont_status.cont_id
    )
  join
    regauth
  on
    regauth.user_id=status.id_publ and regauth.cont_id=117
  where Status.id_rsl<100 and
        Status.dt_tm-Regauth.reg_time>=0 and
        Status.dt_tm-Regauth.reg_time<(Contests.duration-Contests.freeze_time)/24
                and
        Status.dt_tm-Regauth.reg_time<=
           (
             select current_timestamp-reg_time
             from Regauth
             where cont_id=117 and user_id=0
           )

  order by Status.id_publ,
           Cont_prob.pr_num,
           Status.dt_tm

Mon Feb 22 18:36:04 2016:   select R.reg_time+C.duration/24-current_timestamp,

Mon Feb 22 18:36:04 2016: Tmp_stand called: cont_id=117, isteam=0, isvirt=1, user=0, type=1, master=0
Mon Feb 22 18:36:04 2016:   select Status.id_publ, Cont_prob.pr_num, Status.id_rsl,
        (cast(Status.dt_tm as date)-cast(Regauth.reg_time as date))*24*60+
        (cast(Status.dt_tm as time)-cast(Regauth.reg_time as time))/60 penalty
  from
    (
      (
        (status join cont_status on status.id_stat=cont_status.id_stat and cont_status.cont_id=117)
      join
        cont_prob
      on
        cont_prob.prob_id=status.id_prb and cont_status.cont_id=cont_prob.cont_id
      )
    join
      contests
    on
      contests.cont_id=cont_status.cont_id
    )
  join
    regauth
  on
    regauth.user_id=status.id_publ and regauth.cont_id=117
  where Status.id_rsl<100 and
        Status.dt_tm-Regauth.reg_time>=0 and
        Status.dt_tm-Regauth.reg_time<(Contests.duration-Contests.freeze_time)/24
                and
        Status.dt_tm-Regauth.reg_time<=
           (
             select current_timestamp-reg_time
             from Regauth
             where cont_id=117 and user_id=0
           )

  order by Status.id_publ,
           Cont_prob.pr_num,
           Status.dt_tm

Sat Feb 27 15:35:43 2016:   select Status.id_publ, Cont_prob.pr_num, Status.id_rsl,
        (cast(Status.dt_tm as date)-cast(Contests."START" as date))*24*60+

  from
    (

      cont_prob

           Status.dt_tm

Sun Feb 28 23:40:11 2016: Tmp_stand called: cont_id=116, isteam=0, isvirt=1, user=0, type=1, master=0
Sun Feb 28 23:40:11 2016:   select Status.id_publ, Cont_prob.pr_num, Status.id_rsl,
        (cast(Status.dt_tm as date)-cast(Regauth.reg_time as date))*24*60+
        (cast(Status.dt_tm as time)-cast(Regauth.reg_time as time))/60 penalty
  from
    (
      (
        (status join cont_status on status.id_stat=cont_status.id_stat and cont_status.cont_id=116)
      join
        cont_prob
      on
        cont_prob.prob_id=status.id_prb and cont_status.cont_id=cont_prob.cont_id
      )
    join
      contests
    on
      contests.cont_id=cont_status.cont_id
    )
  join
    regauth
  on
    regauth.user_id=status.id_publ and regauth.cont_id=116
  where Status.id_rsl<100 and
        Status.dt_tm-Regauth.reg_time>=0 and
        Status.dt_tm-Regauth.reg_time<(Contests.duration-Contests.freeze_time)/24
                and
        Status.dt_tm-Regauth.reg_time<=
           (
             select current_timestamp-reg_time
             from Regauth
             where cont_id=116 and user_id=0
           )

  order by Status.id_publ,
           Cont_prob.pr_num,
           Status.dt_tm

  from

  where Status.id_rsl<100 and

        Contests.stop-Contests.freeze_time/24-Status.dt_tm>0
